# Diagram: research/orchestrator/tasks/models/partview_spark.py


> Auto-generated by Obscura crawlers

## Diagram 1

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([Start]) --> ParseArgs[Parse Command Line Args<br/>s3_input_path, s3_output_path, env]
    ParseArgs --> InitSpark[Initialize Spark Context<br/>and SQL Context]
    InitSpark --> ReadParquet[Read Parquet from s3_input_path]
    ReadParquet --> FirstGroupBy[Group by multiple dimensions<br/>tl_ids, pc_solution_id, locations, etc.]
    FirstGroupBy --> FirstAgg[Aggregate: countDistinct, avg, stddev<br/>num_containers, transit times]
    FirstAgg --> CalcDeltas[Calculate time deltas<br/>30, 60, 90, 120, 180, 365 days]
    CalcDeltas --> GetModelHierarchy[Get model hierarchy<br/>from model_mapper]
    GetModelHierarchy --> LoopModels{For each model<br/>in hierarchy}
    LoopModels --> GetRollupKeys[Get rollup keys for model]
    GetRollupKeys --> MapFeatures[Map features using<br/>FEATURE_VERSION_MAPPINGS]
    MapFeatures --> ModelGroupBy[Group by mapped rollup keys]
    ModelGroupBy --> TimeWindowAgg[Aggregate statistics for<br/>each time window<br/>mean, stddev, percentiles, counts]
    TimeWindowAgg --> RenameColumns[Rename columns back to<br/>original names]
    RenameColumns --> BuildOutputPath[Build S3 output path<br/>for model]
    BuildOutputPath --> RedisLoad[Load to Redis protocol<br/>redis_bulk_load.rollup_to_redis_protocol]
    RedisLoad --> WriteParquet[Write parquet to<br/>model_output_path]
    WriteParquet --> WriteLatest[Write parquet to<br/>latest path]
    WriteLatest --> MoreModels{More models?}
    MoreModels -->|Yes| LoopModels
    MoreModels -->|No| End([End])
```

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Main
    participant SparkContext
    participant SQLContext
    participant DataFrame
    participant ModelMapper
    participant RedisBulkLoad
    participant S3

    Main->>SparkContext: Initialize Spark
    Main->>SQLContext: Create SQL Context
    Main->>S3: Read parquet(s3_input_path)
    S3-->>DataFrame: Return base_df
    Main->>DataFrame: groupby + agg (first aggregation)
    DataFrame-->>Main: Aggregated base_df
    Main->>Main: Calculate time deltas
    Main->>ModelMapper: Get model_hierarchy
    ModelMapper-->>Main: Return model list
    loop For each model
        Main->>ModelMapper: Get rollup_keys for model
        ModelMapper-->>Main: Return rollup_keys
        Main->>ModelMapper: Map features via FEATURE_VERSION_MAPPINGS
        ModelMapper-->>Main: Return new_rollup_keys
        Main->>DataFrame: groupby(new_rollup_keys) + agg (time windows)
        DataFrame-->>Main: model_rollup
        Main->>DataFrame: Rename columns back to original
        Main->>Main: Build output paths
        Main->>RedisBulkLoad: rollup_to_redis_protocol()
        Main->>S3: Write parquet (model_output_path)
        Main->>S3: Write parquet (latest_out_full)
    end
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph Helper Functions
        A[get_latest_path] --> A1[Remove version from path]
        B[get_s3_output_folder] --> B1[Extract folder from path]
        C[rename_columns_with_prefix] --> C1[Add prefix to all columns]
    end
    
    subgraph Data Processing
        D[Read Parquet] --> E[First Aggregation]
        E --> F[Model Loop]
        F --> G[Time Window Aggregations]
        G --> H[Column Remapping]
        H --> I[Write to S3 + Redis]
    end
    
    subgraph External Dependencies
        J[model_mapper]
        K[redis_bulk_load]
        L[pyspark]
    end
    
    F --> J
    I --> K
    D --> L
    E --> L
    G --> L
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class Main {
        +s3_input_path: str
        +s3_output_path: str
        +env: str
        +main()
    }
    
    class HelperFunctions {
        +get_latest_path(versioned_path)
        +get_s3_output_folder(s3_output_path)
        +rename_columns_with_prefix(df, prefix)
    }
    
    class DataPipeline {
        +base_df: DataFrame
        +model_rollup: DataFrame
        +rollup_keys: list
        +time_deltas: dict
    }
    
    class Aggregations {
        +num_containers
        +transit_std
        +num_obs
        +30_day_mean
        +60_day_mean
        +90_day_mean
        +120_day_mean
        +180_day_mean
        +365_day_mean
        +percentiles
    }
    
    Main --> HelperFunctions
    Main --> DataPipeline
    DataPipeline --> Aggregations
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Initialize
    Initialize --> ReadData: Spark Context Created
    ReadData --> BaseAggregation: Parquet Loaded
    BaseAggregation --> ModelIteration: Base DF Aggregated
    ModelIteration --> GetModelConfig: Start Model Loop
    GetModelConfig --> FeatureMapping: Config Retrieved
    FeatureMapping --> GroupAndAggregate: Features Mapped
    GroupAndAggregate --> ComputeTimeWindows: Grouped by Keys
    ComputeTimeWindows --> ColumnRename: 30/60/90/120/180/365 day stats
    ColumnRename --> OutputPrep: Columns Renamed
    OutputPrep --> RedisWrite: Paths Built
    RedisWrite --> ParquetWrite: Redis Protocol Written
    ParquetWrite --> LatestWrite: Model Parquet Written
    LatestWrite --> CheckMoreModels: Latest Parquet Written
    CheckMoreModels --> GetModelConfig: More Models
    CheckMoreModels --> [*]: No More Models
```
